													$action$_ambient_object = pin_31
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_30
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 29 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_29
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_28
												}
											}
										}
										else = {
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 26 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 27 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_27
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_26
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 25 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_25
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_24
												}
											}
										}
									}
									else = {
										if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 20 } }
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 22 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 23 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_23
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_22
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 21 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_21
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_20
												}
											}
										}
										else = {
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 18 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 19 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_19
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_18
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 17 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_17
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_16
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
								else = {
									if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 8 } }
										if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 12 } }
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 14 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 15 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_15
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_14
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 13 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_13
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_12
												}
											}
										}
										else = {
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 10 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 11 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_11
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_10
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 9 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_9
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_8
												}
											}
										}
									}
									else = {
										if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 4 } }
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 6 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 7 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_7
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_6
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 5 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_5
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_4
												}
											}
										}
										else = {
											if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 2 } }
												if = { limit = { check_key = { lhs = $inp$ value = 3 } }
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_3
												}
												else = {
													$action$_ambient_object = pin_2
												}
											}
											else = {
												$action$_ambient_object = pin_1
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
